>>> from bokeh.plotting import figure
>>> import pandas as pd
>>> d1=pd.read_csv('C:/StockData/Weekly/RELIANCE.NS.csv')
>>> a=[d1['Open'][0],d1['Open'][1]]
>>> def pred2(a,b):
    import pandas as pd
    tmp=[a[b].mean()]
    for i in range(1,a.shape[0]+1):
        tmp.append(tmp[i-1]*0.15+a.loc[i-1][b]*0.85)
    tmp1=[]
    for i in range(a.shape[0]):
       tmp1.append(tmp[i]/a.loc[i][b])
    return sum(tmp1)/len(tmp1)*tmp[-1]

>>> for i in range(2,d1.shape[0]):
	a.append(pred2(d1[0:i],'Open'))

def hell(x):
	d1=pd.read_csv('C:/StockData/Hourly/%s.csv'%x.upper())
	a=[d1['OPEN'][0],d1['OPEN'][1]]
	for i in range(2,d1.shape[0]):
		a.append(pred2(d1[0:i],'Open'))
	p=figure(plot_width=750,plot_height=300)
	p.line([i for i in range(d1.shape[0])],d1['Open'],legend='Real',line_color='green',line_width=2)
	p.line([i for i in range(d1.shape[0])],a,legend='Predicted',line_color='red',line_width=2)
	bokeh_process = subprocess.Popen(
    ['bokeh', 'serve','--allow-websocket-origin=127.0.0.1:5000','C:/Python34/livegraph.py'], stdout=subprocess.PIPE)
	ses=pull_session(app_path='/livegraph')
	ws=autoload_server(None,app_path='/livegraph',session_id=ses.id)
	scr,div=components(p)
	return '''

def hell(x):
	d1=pd.read_csv('C:/StockData/Hourly/%s.csv'%x.upper())
	a=[d1['OPEN'][0],d1['OPEN'][1]]
	for i in range(2,d1.shape[0]):
		a.append(pred2(d1[0:i],'OPEN'))
	p=figure(plot_width=750,plot_height=300)
	p.line([i for i in range(d1.shape[0])],d1['OPEN'],legend='Real',line_color='green',line_width=2)
	p.line([i for i in range(d1.shape[0])],a,legend='Predicted',line_color='red',line_width=2)
	bokeh_process = subprocess.Popen(
    ['bokeh', 'serve','--allow-websocket-origin=127.0.0.1:5000','C:/Python34/livegraph.py'], stdout=subprocess.PIPE)
	ses=pull_session(app_path='/livegraph')
